    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.3pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><span style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">By:</span><span style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;"> </span></p></td>
    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;border-bottom:0.25pt solid;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.3pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><span style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">/s/ Adam M. Veness, Esq.</span></p></td>

  <title>EX-99.1</title>

 <body style="margin: auto!important;padding: 8px;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.3in;min-height:1in;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><img src="img85518887_0.jpg" alt="img85518887_0.jpg" style="width:290px;height:55px;">&#160;</p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#741b47;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">DIANTHUS THERAPEUTICS HIGHLIGHTS RECENT BUSINESS ACHIEVEMENTS</font><font style="color:#741b47;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#741b47;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">AND REPORTS Q2 FINANCIAL RESULTS</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 MaGic trial in generalized Myasthenia Gravis (gMG) ongoing;</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">  </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">top-line results anticipated in 2H&#x2019;25</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">IND for Phase 2 MoMeNtum trial in Multifocal Motor Neuropathy (MMN) cleared by FDA in June;</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">top-line results anticipated in 2H&#x2019;26</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 trial in Chronic Inflammatory Demyelinating Polyneuropathy (CIDP) to initiate 2H&#x2019;24</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Approximately $361 million of cash provides runway into 2H&#x2019;27</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">New York City and Waltham, Mass., August 8, 2024</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> &#x2013; Dianthus Therapeutics, Inc. (Nasdaq: DNTH), a clinical-stage biotechnology company dedicated to advancing the next generation of antibody complement therapeutics to treat severe autoimmune diseases, today reported financial results for the second quarter ending June 30, 2024, and provided an update on recent business achievements.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;The second quarter of 2024 highlighted the Dianthus team&#x2019;s continued focus on execution and operational excellence as we advance our clinical programs for DNTH103 in generalized Myasthenia Gravis, Multifocal Motor Neuropathy, and Chronic Inflammatory Demyelinating Polyneuropathy,&#x201d; said Marino Garcia, Chief Executive Officer of Dianthus Therapeutics. &#x201c;We believe DNTH103 may be a potentially best-in-class, potent classical complement pathway inhibitor with infrequent, subcutaneous self-administration and a differentiated safety profile across our three initial indications of gMG, MMN and CIDP. We continue to be confident in the pipeline-in-a-product potential of DNTH103 across multiple autoimmune diseases, supported by our proof-of-concept </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">in vitro</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> data presented at EAN and recent competitor clinical data that further validate targeting the classical pathway and active C1s.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Recent Business Highlights and Upcoming Milestones</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103 is an investigational, clinical-stage, potent monoclonal antibody engineered to selectively target the classical pathway by inhibiting only the active form of the C1s protein, a clinically validated complement target. DNTH103 is enhanced with YTE half-life extension technology designed to enable a more convenient subcutaneous, self-administered injection dosed as infrequently as once every two weeks. DNTH103 has the potential to be a best-in-class pipeline-in-a-product across a range of autoimmune disorders with high unmet need.</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div class="page-node-content"><div style="flex-direction:column;display:flex;padding-bottom:0.3in;min-height:1in;justify-content:flex-end;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:0.25in;text-align:right;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">1</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:0.25in;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">www.dianthustx.com 7 Times Square, Floor 43 New York, NY 10036</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:0.25in;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div></div>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.3in;min-height:1in;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 MaGic gMG trial ongoing:</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> The </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">MaGic trial </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">is a global, randomized, double-blind, placebo-controlled Phase 2 study in patients with gMG who are acetylcholine receptor (AChR) antibody positive. Initial top-line results from this trial are anticipated to be available in the second half of 2025.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 IND cleared for MoMeNtum MMN trial: </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">The </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">MoMeNtum trial</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> is a global, randomized, double-blind, placebo-controlled Phase 2 study designed to evaluate the safety, tolerability, and efficacy of DNTH103 in patients with MMN. Initial top-line results from this trial are anticipated to be available in the second half of 2026.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">One oral presentation highlighted DNTH103 at AAN 2024:</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> An </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">oral presentation</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">at the American Academy of Neurology (AAN) Annual Meeting in Denver highlighted preclinical and </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">in vitro</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> data describing the differentiated safety profile and neurotransmission activity of DNTH103 and a review of previously released Phase 1 healthy volunteer data.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Two DNTH103 posters presented at EAN 2024: </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Two </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">poster presentations</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> at the 10th Congress of the European Academy of Neurology (EAN) in Helsinki highlighted preclinical and </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">in vitro</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> data describing the potentially differentiated profile of DNTH103 in disease models of gMG and CIDP, in addition to head-to-head affinity and pharmacodynamic (PD) potency data for DNTH103 compared to riliprubart.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Planning for CIDP Phase 2 trial ongoing: </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Dianthus remains on track to initiate a Phase 2 trial of DNTH103 in CIDP in the second half of 2024.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Corporate</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Effective July 1, 2024, Alison Lawton was appointed Chair of the Dianthus Therapeutics Board of Directors. She succeeded Lonnie Moulder, who remains on the Board of Directors.  </font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Second-Quarter 2024 Financial Results</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Cash Position</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> - $360.7 million of cash, cash equivalents and short-term investments as of June 30, 2024 is projected to provide runway into the second half of 2027.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">R&amp;D Expenses</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> - Research and development (R&amp;D) expenses for the quarter ended June 30, 2024 were $18.1 million, inclusive of $1.4 million of stock-based compensation, compared to $10.3 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2023, which included $0.1 million of stock-based compensation. This increase in R&amp;D expenses was primarily driven by higher clinical costs, chemistry, manufacturing and controls (CMC) costs and increased headcount to support DNTH103 Phase 1 and Phase 2 development.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">G&amp;A Expenses</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> - General and administrative (G&amp;A) expenses for the quarter ended June 30, 2024 totaled $6.0 million, inclusive of stock-based compensation of $1.8 million, compared to $2.5 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2023, which included $0.3 million of stock-based compensation. This increase in G&amp;A expenses was primarily due to higher headcount and consulting and professional fees.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.333%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Net Loss</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> - Net loss for the quarter ended June 30, 2024 was $17.6 million or $0.51 per share (basic and diluted) compared to $11.1 million or $12.73 per share (basic and diluted) for the quarter ended June 30, 2023.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="page-node-content"><div style="flex-direction:column;display:flex;padding-bottom:0.3in;min-height:1in;justify-content:flex-end;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:0.25in;text-align:right;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">2</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:0.25in;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">www.dianthustx.com 7 Times Square, Floor 43 New York, NY 10036</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:0.25in;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div></div>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.3in;min-height:1in;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">About DNTH103</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"><br></font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103 is an investigational, clinical-stage, potent monoclonal antibody engineered to selectively target the classical pathway by inhibiting only the active form of the C1s protein, a clinically validated complement target. DNTH103 is enhanced with YTE half-life extension technology designed to enable a more convenient subcutaneous, self-administered injection dosed as infrequently as once every two weeks. Additionally, selective inhibition of the classical complement pathway may lower patient risk of infection from encapsulated bacteria by preserving immune activity of the lectin and alternative pathways. As the classical pathway plays a significant role in disease pathology, DNTH103 has the potential to be a best-in-class pipeline-in-a-product across a range of autoimmune disorders with high unmet need. Dianthus is building a neuromuscular franchise with DNTH103 following the initiation of the Phase 2 MaGic trial in generalized Myasthenia Gravis in 1Q&#x2019;24, regulatory clearance for Multifocal Motor Neuropathy in 2Q&#x2019;24, and planned initiation of a Phase 2 trial in Chronic Inflammatory Demyelinating Polyneuropathy in 2H&#x2019;24.</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103 is an investigational agent that is not approved as a therapy in any indication in any jurisdiction worldwide.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">About Dianthus Therapeutics</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Dianthus Therapeutics is a clinical-stage biotechnology company dedicated to designing and delivering novel, best-in-class monoclonal antibodies with improved selectivity and potency. Based in New York City and Waltham, Mass., Dianthus is comprised of an experienced team of biotech and pharma executives who are leading the development of next-generation antibody complement therapeutics, aiming to deliver transformative medicines for people living with severe autoimmune and inflammatory diseases.</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">To learn more, please visit </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">www.dianthustx.com </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">and follow us on </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">LinkedIn</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></p>
